double distance(pair<int, int> a, pair<int, int> b) {
	int x1, x2, y1, y2;
	x1 = a.first;
	x2 = b.first;
	y1 = a.second;
	y2 = b.second;
	return sqrt(pow(x1 - x2, 2) + pow(y1 - y2, 2));
}

		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, -8));

		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, -6));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, -5));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, -4));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, -3));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, -2));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, -1));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, 0));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, 1));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, 2));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, 3));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, 4));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, 5));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, 6));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, 7));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, 8));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(49, 9));
		newPoints.push_back(make_pair(50, 0));
	}

	int itemp;
	int itemp1;
	char ctemp;

	for (int testcase = 1; testcase <= 1; testcase++) {
		// resets variables
		existingHouses.clear();
		democratNum = 0;

		// takes center of new house
		input >> itemp;
		input >> itemp1;
		centerNew = make_pair(itemp, itemp1);

		for (pair<int, int> thisLoc : newPoints) {
			thisLoc.first += centerNew.first;
			thisLoc.second += centerNew.second;
		}

		// takes all existing houses
		for (int i = 1; i <= 20; i++) {
			input >> itemp;
			input >> itemp1;
			input >> ctemp;
			existingHouses.push_back(make_pair(make_pair(itemp, itemp1), ctemp));
		}

		// takes all possible locations
		for (pair<int, int> thisLoc : newPoints) {
			for (pair<pair<int, int>, char> exHouse : existingHouses) {
				topHouses.push_back(make_pair(distance(thisLoc, exHouse.first), exHouse.second));
			}
			// sorts top houses
			sort(topHouses.begin(), topHouses.end());

			// initializes vector of voting houses
			voteHouses.push_back(topHouses[0].second);
			voteHouses.push_back(topHouses[1].second);
			voteHouses.push_back(topHouses[2].second);
			for (int i = 3; i < 100; i++) {
				if (topHouses[i].first == topHouses[2].first) {
					voteHouses.push_back(topHouses[i].second);
				}
			}

			int dem = 0;
			int rep = 0;
			for (char a : voteHouses) {
				if (a == 'D') {
					dem++;
				}
				else if (a == 'R') {
					rep++;
				}
			}

			if (rep > dem) {
			}
			else {
				democratNum++;
			}
		}
		output.push_back(democratNum / newHouseLoc);
	}

	for (double e : output) {
		cout << e << endl;
	}

	return 0;
}
